# DIS Enumerations
# This file maps from a dis entity type to a platform type name.  The platform type
# name is used to create an 'informative' platform name in cases where none is
# provided.  If you are interested in changing the model mappings, please see the
# dis_map.dat file instead.
#
# The DIS entity type takes the following form:
# A:B:C:D:E:F:G
# where
# A - represents an entity kind
# B - represents a domain
# C - represents the country of origin
# D - represents a category
# E - represents a sub-category
# F - is a specific identifier
# G - is a extra identifier
#
# Entity Kind:
# 1 - Platform
# 2 - Munition
#
# Country of origin:
# 0   - Terrorist / Unaffiliated
# 2   - Albania
# 10  - Argentina
# 13  - Australia
# 15  - Bahamas
# 16  - Bahrain
# 21  - Belgium
# 22  - Belize
# 24  - Bermuda
# 39  - Canada
# 45  - People's Republic of China
# 55  - Cyprus
# 56  - Czechoslovakia
# 57  - Denmark
# 62  - Egypt
# 71  - France
# 78  - German
# 82  - Greece
# 99  - India
# 101 - Iran
# 102 - Iraq
# 105 - Israel
# 106 - Italy
# 110 - Japan
# 114 - Jordan
# 119 - Democratic People's Republic of Korea (North Korea)
# 120 - Republic of Korea (South Korea)
# 121 - Kuwait
# 123 - Lebanon
# 125 - Liberia
# 126 - Libya
# 153 - Netherlands
# 163 - Norway
# 164 - Oman
# 165 - Pakistan
# 168 - Panama
# 173 - Philippines
# 178 - Qatar
# 189 - Saudi Arabia
# 193 - Singapore
# 197 - South Africa
# 198 - Spain
# 205 - Sweden
# 206 - Switzerland
# 208 - Taiwan
# 210 - Thailand
# 218 - Turkey
# 222 - CIS (Russia)
# 223 - United Arab Emirates
# 224 - UK
# 225 - USA
# 237 - Yemen
# 240 - Yugoslavia
# 249 - Crocia
#
# Platform Domains
# 0  - Ground
# 1  - Air
# 2  - Sea
# 4  - Submarine
# 5  - Space
#
# Munition Domains
# 0  - Other
# 1  - Anti-air
# 2  - Anti-armor
# 3  - Anti-guided-weapon
# 4  - Anti-radar
# 5  - Anti-satellite
# 6  - Anti-ship
# 7  - Anti-submarine
# 8  - Anti-personnel
# 9  - Battlefield Support
# 10 - Strategic
# 11 - Tactical
# 12 - Directed Energy
#
